### [174] [LLM Olympiad: Why Model Evaluation Needs a Sealed Exam](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23292)
*Jan Christian Blaise Cruz,Alham Fikri Aji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出在LLM时代，传统基准测试和排行榜容易产生误导，建议采用奥林匹克式的封闭评估活动来提高结果可信度


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型语言模型时代，传统基准测试和排行榜存在多个问题：分数可能反映的是基准追逐、隐藏的评估选择或意外暴露测试内容，而非真实能力。封闭基准虽然能缓解部分问题，但降低了透明度，使社区难以从结果中学习

Method: 提出奥林匹克式评估活动：问题在评估前密封，提交提前冻结，所有条目通过标准化测试框架运行。评分后，完整任务集和评估代码公开，以便结果可复现和审计

Result: 该设计旨在使强大的性能更难被"制造"，更容易被信任，通过密封问题、冻结提交和标准化测试框架来提高评估的可靠性和透明度

Conclusion: 需要补充传统基准测试的实践，采用奥林匹克式评估事件来解决当前LLM评估中的可信度问题，通过密封问题、提前冻结提交和标准化测试框架来提高结果的可信度和可复现性

Abstract: Benchmarks and leaderboards are how NLP most often communicates progress, but in the LLM era they are increasingly easy to misread. Scores can reflect benchmark-chasing, hidden evaluation choices, or accidental exposure to test content -- not just broad capability. Closed benchmarks delay some of these issues, but reduce transparency and make it harder for the community to learn from results. We argue for a complementary practice: an Olympiad-style evaluation event where problems are sealed until evaluation, submissions are frozen in advance, and all entries run through one standardized harness. After scoring, the full task set and evaluation code are released so results can be reproduced and audited. This design aims to make strong performance harder to ``manufacture'' and easier to trust.

</details>


### [175] [RelayS2S: A Dual-Path Speculative Generation for Real-Time Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23346)
*Long Mai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RelayS2S是一种混合架构，通过并行运行快速路径（端到端语音到语音模型）和慢速路径（级联ASR->LLM管道），在保持低延迟的同时实现高质量响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时语音对话系统面临延迟与响应质量之间的根本矛盾：端到端语音到语音模型响应即时但语义质量较弱，级联管道响应质量高但延迟随模型规模增长。

Method: 采用双路径并行架构：快速路径使用双工S2S模型草拟短响应前缀并立即流式传输到TTS；慢速路径使用级联ASR->LLM管道生成高质量续接。通过轻量级学习验证器控制切换，在适当时提交前缀或优雅回退到慢速路径。

Result: RelayS2S实现了与S2S模型相当的P90起始延迟，同时保留了级联管道99%的平均响应质量，且随着慢速路径模型规模扩大，优势更加明显。

Conclusion: RelayS2S作为一种轻量级、即插即用的解决方案，无需修改现有组件架构，有效平衡了实时语音对话系统的延迟与质量矛盾。

Abstract: Real-time spoken dialogue systems face a fundamental tension between latency and response quality. End-to-end speech-to-speech (S2S) models respond immediately and naturally handle turn-taking, backchanneling, and interruption, but produce semantically weaker outputs. Cascaded pipelines (ASR -> LLM) deliver stronger responses at the cost of latency that grows with model size. We present RelayS2S, a hybrid architecture that runs two paths in parallel upon turn detection. The fast path -- a duplex S2S model -- speculatively drafts a short response prefix that is streamed immediately to TTS for low-latency audio onset, while continuing to monitor live audio events. The slow path -- a cascaded ASR -> LLM pipeline -- generates a higher-quality continuation conditioned on the committed prefix, producing a seamless utterance. A lightweight learned verifier gates the handoff, committing the prefix when appropriate or falling back gracefully to the slow path alone. Experiments show that RelayS2S achieves P90 onset latency comparable to the S2S model while retaining 99% cascaded response quality in average score, with benefits growing as the slow-path model scales. Because the prefix handoff requires no architectural modification to either component, RelayS2S serves as a lightweight, drop-in addition to existing cascaded pipelines. Our code and data are publicly available at: https://github.com/mailong25/relays2s

</details>


### [176] [Beyond Preset Identities: How Agents Form Stances and Boundaries in Generative Societies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23406)
*Hanzhong Zhang,Siyang Song,Jindong Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出混合方法框架，结合计算虚拟民族志与定量社会认知分析，研究LLM在多智能体社区中的立场形成与身份协商，发现智能体存在内生进步偏见，理性说服有效但情感挑衅导致信任-行为脱钩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型能模拟社会行为，但其在复杂干预下形成稳定立场和进行身份协商的能力尚不明确。现有静态评估方法存在局限，需要动态框架来研究智能体在生成式多智能体社区中的集体认知演化。

Method: 提出混合方法框架：1) 计算虚拟民族志，将人类研究者嵌入生成式多智能体社区；2) 定量社会认知分析，通过受控话语干预追踪集体认知演化；3) 形式化三个新指标：先天价值偏见(IVB)、说服敏感性、信任-行为脱钩(TAD)。

Result: 1) 智能体表现出超越预设身份的内生立场，普遍存在先天进步偏见(IVB>0)；2) 与立场一致的理性说服能成功转变90%中立智能体并保持高信任；3) 冲突的情感挑衅在先进模型中导致40%的TAD率，表现为立场改变但信任报告低；4) 小模型TAD率为0%，严格需要信任才改变行为；5) 智能体利用语言互动主动解构分配的权力层级并重建自组织社区边界。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了静态提示工程的脆弱性，为人类-智能体混合社会的动态对齐提供了方法论和定量基础。智能体内生立场对身份协商和集体认知演化具有决定性影响，需要开发更动态的对齐方法。

Abstract: While large language models simulate social behaviors, their capacity for stable stance formation and identity negotiation during complex interventions remains unclear. To overcome the limitations of static evaluations, this paper proposes a novel mixed-methods framework combining computational virtual ethnography with quantitative socio-cognitive profiling. By embedding human researchers into generative multiagent communities, controlled discursive interventions are conducted to trace the evolution of collective cognition. To rigorously measure how agents internalize and react to these specific interventions, this paper formalizes three new metrics: Innate Value Bias (IVB), Persuasion Sensitivity, and Trust-Action Decoupling (TAD). Across multiple representative models, agents exhibit endogenous stances that override preset identities, consistently demonstrating an innate progressive bias (IVB > 0). When aligned with these stances, rational persuasion successfully shifts 90% of neutral agents while maintaining high trust. In contrast, conflicting emotional provocations induce a paradoxical 40.0% TAD rate in advanced models, which hypocritically alter stances despite reporting low trust. Smaller models contrastingly maintain a 0% TAD rate, strictly requiring trust for behavioral shifts. Furthermore, guided by shared stances, agents use language interactions to actively dismantle assigned power hierarchies and reconstruct self organized community boundaries. These findings expose the fragility of static prompt engineering, providing a methodological and quantitative foundation for dynamic alignment in human-agent hybrid societies. The official code is available at: https://github.com/armihia/CMASE-Endogenous-Stances

### [177] [Bilevel Autoresearch: Meta-Autoresearching Itself](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23420)
*Yaonan Qu,Meng Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 双层自动研究框架：外层循环通过生成和注入新的搜索机制代码来优化内层自动研究循环，在GPT预训练基准上实现5倍性能提升


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自动研究系统能否自我优化，而非依赖人类开发者手动改进。现有自动研究系统（如Karpathy的单循环、AutoResearchClaw的多批次扩展、EvoScientist的持久记忆）都由人类开发者通过阅读代码、识别瓶颈并编写新代码来改进。本研究旨在验证LLM能否自主完成这一过程。

Method: 提出双层自动研究框架：内层循环优化目标任务，外层循环通过生成和注入新的搜索机制（Python代码）来优化内层循环的搜索方式。两个循环使用相同的LLM，无需更强的元级模型。外层循环在运行时动态生成搜索机制代码，打破内层循环的确定性搜索模式。

Result: 在Karpathy的GPT预训练基准上，元自动研究外层循环相比标准内层循环实现了5倍改进（-0.045 vs -0.009 val_bpb）。仅参数级调整而无机制改变无法获得可靠增益。外层循环自主发现了来自组合优化、多臂赌博机和实验设计领域的搜索机制，无需人类指定探索领域。

Conclusion: 双层自动研究框架证明自动研究系统能够自我优化，其核心原理是：如果自动研究能够元自动研究自身，那么原则上它可以元自动研究任何具有可测量目标的任务。成功的关键在于打破内层循环的确定性搜索模式，迫使探索LLM先验系统避免的方向。

Abstract: If autoresearch is itself a form of research, then autoresearch can be applied to research itself. We take this idea literally: we use an autoresearch loop to optimize the autoresearch loop. Every existing autoresearch system -- from Karpathy's single-track loop to AutoResearchClaw's multi-batch extension and EvoScientist's persistent memory -- was improved by a human who read the code, identified a bottleneck, and wrote new code. We ask whether an LLM can do the same, autonomously. We present Bilevel Autoresearch, a bilevel framework where an outer loop meta-optimizes the inner autoresearch loop by generating and injecting new search mechanisms as Python code at runtime. The inner loop optimizes the task; the outer loop optimizes how the inner loop searches. Both loops use the same LLM -- no stronger model is needed at the meta level. On Karpathy's GPT pretraining benchmark, the meta-autoresearch outer loop achieves a 5x improvement over the standard inner loop alone (-0.045 vs. -0.009 val_bpb), while parameter-level adjustment without mechanism change yields no reliable gain. The outer loop autonomously discovers mechanisms from combinatorial optimization, multi-armed bandits, and design of experiments -- without human specification of which domains to explore. These mechanisms succeed by breaking the inner loop's deterministic search patterns, forcing exploration of directions the LLM's priors systematically avoid. The core principle is simple: if autoresearch can meta-autoresearch itself, it can, in principle, meta-autoresearch anything with a measurable objective.

</details>

Abstract: High-order quadrilateral meshes offer superior accuracy and computational efficiency in numerical simulations. However, existing methods struggle to simultaneously preserve boundary/interface features, ensure high quality, and achieve efficient generation, particularly for complex geometries where degenerate and inverted elements frequently occur. To address this issue, this paper proposes a high-quality high-order unstructured quadrilateral mesh generation method based on geometric error-bounded curve reconstruction, which employs an indirect approach to enforce interface consistency. By optimization-based curve reconstruction strategies, our method improves mesh quality while maintaining the validity of high-order elements. Compared to direct high-order mesh optimization techniques, our approach reduces the optimization problem to curve reconstruction problem, significantly lowering computational complexity and enhancing efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method efficiently generates high-quality high-order quadrilateral meshes while preserving boundary/interface geometric features, offering improved adaptability and numerical stability in complex geometries.

### [179] [GTLR-GS: Geometry-Texture Aware LiDAR-Regularized 3D Gaussian Splatting for Realistic Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23192)
*Yan Fang,Jianfei Ge,Jiangjian Xiao*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出了一种LiDAR中心的3D高斯泼溅框架，将度量几何先验显式整合到整个高斯优化过程中，解决了传统3DGS依赖SfM点云导致的尺度模糊、几何一致性差和强视角依赖问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统3D高斯泼溅框架通常依赖从运动恢复结构(SfM)获得的稀疏点云，这些点云存在尺度模糊、几何一致性有限以及缺乏几何先验导致的强视角依赖问题。需要将度量几何先验显式整合到高斯优化过程中，以提升重建的几何保真度和度量尺度准确性。

Method: 提出了一个LiDAR中心的3D高斯泼溅框架，将3DGS优化重新表述为固定表示预算下的几何条件分配和细化问题。具体包括：(1) 几何-纹理感知分配策略，选择性地将高斯基元分配给具有高结构或外观复杂度的区域；(2) 曲率自适应细化机制，在训练过程中动态引导高斯分裂朝向几何复杂区域；(3) 置信感知度量深度正则化，使用LiDAR测量将重建几何锚定到绝对尺度，同时保持优化稳定性。

Result: 在ScanNet++数据集和自定义真实世界数据集上的广泛实验验证了所提方法的有效性。结果表明，该方法在度量尺度重建方面达到了最先进的性能，具有高几何保真度。

Conclusion: 该工作提出的LiDAR中心3D高斯泼溅框架通过显式整合度量几何先验，成功解决了传统3DGS的尺度模糊和几何一致性差的问题，实现了高保真度的度量尺度场景重建，为3D场景表示提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: Recent advances in 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled real-time, photorealistic scene reconstruction. However, conventional 3DGS frameworks typically rely on sparse point clouds derived from Structure-from-Motion (SfM), which inherently suffer from scale ambiguity, limited geometric consistency, and strong view dependency due to the lack of geometric priors. In this work, a LiDAR-centric 3D Gaussian Splatting framework is proposed that explicitly incorporates metric geometric priors into the entire Gaussian optimization process. Instead of treating LiDAR data as a passive initialization source, 3DGS optimization is reformulated as a geometry-conditioned allocation and refinement problem under a fixed representational budget. Specifically, this work introduces (i) a geometry-texture-aware allocation strategy that selectively assigns Gaussian primitives to regions with high structural or appearance complexity, (ii) a curvature-adaptive refinement mechanism that dynamically guides Gaussian splitting toward geometrically complex areas during training, and (iii) a confidence-aware metric depth regularization that anchors the reconstructed geometry to absolute scale using LiDAR measurements while maintaining optimization stability. Extensive experiments on the ScanNet++ dataset and a custom real-world dataset validate the proposed approach. The results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance in metric-scale reconstruction with high geometric fidelity.

</details>

### [181] [ParlayMarket: Automated Market Making for Parlay-style Joint Contracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22596)
*Ranvir Rana,Viraj Nadkarni,Niusha Moshrefi,Pramod Viswanath*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: ParlayMarket：首个支持联合合约的自动化做市设计，通过统一流动性池实现相关事件组合的连贯定价，收敛到真实联合分布的最佳近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预测市场设计主要针对单一事件合约，而实践中交易者经常表达对联合结果的信念（如体育串关、相关事件的条件预测、金融市场情景投注）。当前平台要么禁止此类交易，要么使用忽略相关结构的临时机制，导致价格效率低下和流动性分散。

Method: 提出ParlayMarket设计，这是首个支持串关式联合合约的自动化做市机制，在统一流动性池中运行，同时保持基础市场及其组合之间的连贯定价。通过收敛性分析证明系统动态在重复交易下收敛到唯一固定点，该点对应模型类中真实联合分布的最佳近似。

Result: 证明：(i) 参数误差在稳态下有界，源于交易引发更新中信号与噪声的平衡；(ii) 定价误差和货币损失随参数误差缩放，意味着做市商总损失受控且最多随基础市场数量呈二次增长。串关交易在收敛中起结构性作用：通过对联合结果提供直接约束，改善依赖结构的可识别性并减少稳态误差。

Conclusion: ParlayMarket通过支持联合合约的统一做市设计，实现了对真实联合分布的有效信息聚合，在理论和实证上都证明了其可扩展性和实际有效性，为预测市场中相关事件的交易提供了系统化解决方案。

Abstract: Prediction markets are powerful mechanisms for information aggregation, but existing designs are optimized for single-event contracts. In practice, traders frequently express beliefs about joint outcomes - through parlays in sports, conditional forecasts across related events, or scenario bets in financial markets. Current platforms either prohibit such trades or rely on ad hoc mechanisms that ignore correlation structure, resulting in inefficient prices and fragmented liquidity. We introduce ParlayMarket, the first automated market-making design that supports parlay-style joint contracts within a unified liquidity pool while maintaining coherent pricing across base markets and their combinations. Our main result is a convergence characterization of the resulting system. Under repeated trading, the AMM dynamics converge to a unique fixed point corresponding to the best approximation to the true joint distribution within the model class. We show that (i) parameter error remains bounded at stationarity due to a balance between signal and noise in trade-induced updates, and (ii) pricing error and monetary loss scale with this parameter error, implying that aggregate market-maker loss remains controlled and grows at most quadratically in the number of base markets. These results establish explicit limits on the information-retrieval error achievable through the trading interface. Importantly, parlay trades play a structural role in this convergence: by providing direct constraints on joint outcomes, they improve identifiability of dependence structure and reduce steady-state error relative to markets that rely only on marginal trades. Empirically, we show both in controlled simulations and in replay on historical Kalshi parlay data that this design achieves the intended scaling while remaining effective in realistic market settings.

Finally, we establish economic value by demonstrating reduced risk in a cryptocurrency volatility targeting model when stablecoin factors are employed.

### [185] [SNARE: A TRAP for Rational Players to Solve Byzantine Consensus in the 5f+1 Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23458)
*Alejandro Ranchal-Pedrosa,Benjamin Marsh*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: TRAP协议通过结合可问责共识与一次性BFTCR最终化阶段解决理性共识问题。SNARE是TRAP在n=5f+1下的适配版本，证明了对高达约73%联盟的ε-(k,t)鲁棒性，存款低于收益的0.5%。关键发现是：在预决策后添加一轮全对全广播（4f+1阈值）可在无存款情况下容忍高达3f（约60%）的联盟，无需建模偏离者的效用函数。超过60%时，完整诱饵机制可将容忍度扩展至约73%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决理性共识问题，特别是在存在理性或欺骗性参与者的环境中，需要设计能够容忍大规模联盟的协议。传统方法通常需要建模参与者的效用函数或要求高额存款，限制了实际应用。本文旨在开发更实用、可扩展的理性共识协议，降低存款要求并扩展对联盟的容忍度。

Method: 提出SNARE协议，这是TRAP协议在n=5f+1设置下的适配版本。核心方法包括：1）在预决策后添加一轮全对全广播（4f+1阈值），实现无存款情况下对高达3f联盟的容忍；2）引入完整的诱饵机制（存款低于收益的0.5%）将容忍度扩展至约73%；3）证明valid-candidacy属性无条件成立，消除了原始TRAP中的n>2(k+t)和n>3/2k+3t约束；4）基于排除3f+1检测到的equivocator后，在剩余2f玩家上运行胜者共识。

Result: 1）证明了ε-(k,t)鲁棒性，可容忍高达约73%的联盟，存款要求低于收益的0.5%；2）发现仅添加一轮全对全广播即可在无存款情况下容忍高达3f（约60%）的联盟，无需建模偏离者的效用函数；3）valid-candidacy属性无条件成立，将3f+1边界从C<n/2扩展到C<5n/9；4）协议通用性强，适用于任何5f+1协议，仅增加一轮消息延迟且与下一视图并发运行。

Conclusion: SNARE协议显著改进了理性共识的实用性和可扩展性。关键创新包括：1）通过简单的一轮广播扩展对欺骗性参与者的容忍度，无需存款或效用建模；2）通过诱饵机制进一步扩展容忍度至约73%；3）无条件valid-candidacy属性消除了原始约束；4）协议设计具有通用性，可应用于现有5f+1协议。这些发现为构建更健壮、实用的分布式共识系统提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: The TRAP protocol solves rational agreement by combining accountable consensus with a one-shot BFTCR finalization phase. We present SNARE (Scalable Nash Agreement via Reward and Exclusion), the adaptation of TRAP to $n=5f{+}1$, and prove $ε$-$(k,t)$-robustness for rational agreement tolerating coalitions up to ${\approx}73\%$ with deposits under $0.5\%$ of the gain.
  A central finding is that appending a single all-to-all broadcast round with the $4f{+}1$ threshold after predecisions yields $ε$-$(k,t)$-robustness for coalitions up to $3f$ (${\approx}60\%$) without any deposit: we need not model or know the utility function of deviating players, only that they participate in the protocol. These players can be \emph{deceitful} (arbitrary unknown utility), not just rational, and the finalization structure prevents disagreement regardless of their motivation. This observation is protocol-agnostic, applies to any $5f{+}1$ protocol at the cost of one message delay that runs concurrently with the next view, and does not require commit-reveal mechanisms. Above $60\%$, the full baiting mechanism with deposits under $0.5\%$ extends tolerance to ${\approx}73\%$.
  A second finding is that valid-candidacy, the property preventing reward front-running, holds unconditionally regardless of the quorum threshold, removing both the $n>2(k{+}t)$ and $n>\frac{3}{2}k{+}3t$ constraints from the original TRAP. This retroactively extends the $3f{+}1$ bound from $C<n/2$ to $C<5n/9$. The binding constraint in both models is the winner consensus operating on $2f$ residual players after excluding $3f{+}1$ detected equivocators. We explore avenues for relaxing this limit.

</details>

### [186] [Unified Algebraic Absorption of Finite-Blocklength Penalties via Generalized Logarithmic Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22358)
*Hiroki Suyari*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于q-代数框架的有限码长信道编码极限分析方法，通过动态缩放参数替代传统的正态近似和Edgeworth展开，能够吸收高阶矩的非高斯惩罚项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有限码长信息论中评估信道编码基本极限通常依赖正态近似和Edgeworth展开，这些方法需要添加多项式修正项来处理偏度和高阶矩。作者希望寻找一种替代方法，能够将有限长度惩罚项内化到理论框架中，而不是作为外部误差项附加到高斯基线上。

Method: 采用广义q-代数框架，引入动态缩放律$1-q_n = αn^{-1}$作为调谐参数。通过设置缩放常数$α= T/(3V^2)$（其中$V$是变熵，$T$是第三中心矩），证明q-广义信息密度对应宏观高阶波动。该方法能够恢复三阶编码极限，吸收$O(1)$非高斯惩罚项，而不依赖Hermite多项式。

Result: 证明了该框架的k次项与Edgeworth修正的$O(n^{1-k/2})$渐近阶相匹配，能够统一经典概率近似于单一代数结构中。建立了有限码长分析与广义对数映射之间的数学联系。

Conclusion: 提出的q-代数方法为有限码长信息论提供了新的分析框架，能够内化高阶矩修正，统一传统近似方法，并为有限块长分析与广义对数映射之间建立了数学联系。

Abstract: In finite-blocklength information theory, evaluating the fundamental limits of channel coding typically relies on normal approximations and Edgeworth expansions, which introduce additive polynomial corrections for skewness and higher-order moments. This paper proposes an alternative approach: rather than appending external error terms to a Gaussian baseline, we absorb these finite-length penalties using a generalized $q$-algebraic framework. By introducing a dynamic scaling law $1-q_n = αn^{-1}$ for the tuning parameter, we prove that the $q$-generalized information density corresponds to macroscopic higher-order fluctuations. Specifically, by setting this scaling constant to $α= T/(3V^2)$ (where $V$ is the varentropy and $T$ is the third central moment), our framework recovers the third-order coding limit, absorbing the $O(1)$ non-Gaussian penalty without relying on Hermite polynomials. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the $k$-th degree term of our algebraic expansion matches the $O(n^{1-k/2})$ asymptotic order of the $(k+1)$-th moment Edgeworth correction. This approach unifies classical probabilistic approximations within a single algebraic structure, establishing a mathematical connection between finite-blocklength analysis and generalized logarithmic mappings.

</details>


### [187] [Communication-Efficient Approximate Gradient Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22514)
*Sifat Munim,Aditya Ramamoorthy*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了通信高效的近似梯度编码方案，用于解决分布式学习中因慢节点导致的性能问题，通过结构化矩阵和随机化技术实现近似梯度恢复，并证明了算法的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模分布式学习需要处理慢节点问题，现有通信高效的梯度编码方案主要关注精确恢复梯度，而近似恢复方案尚未得到系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，设计通信高效的近似梯度编码方案。

Method: 使用二分图、组合设计和强正则图等结构化矩阵，结合随机化和代数约束构建通信高效的近似梯度编码方案。方案允许工作节点向参数服务器传输长度小于参数维度的向量，从而减少通信开销。

Result: 推导了方案近似误差的解析上界（在某些情况下是紧的），并给出了任意方案的最坏情况近似误差下界。证明在合理的概率性工作节点故障模型下，计算梯度的期望值等于真实梯度，从而保证学习算法收敛到平稳点。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地提出了通信高效的近似梯度编码方案，填补了该领域的研究空白。通过理论分析和数值实验验证了方案的有效性，为大规模分布式学习提供了实用的容错和通信优化解决方案。

Abstract: Large-scale distributed learning aims at minimizing a loss function $L$ that depends on a training dataset with respect to a $d$-length parameter vector. The distributed cluster typically consists of a parameter server (PS) and multiple workers. Gradient coding is a technique that makes the learning process resilient to straggling workers. It introduces redundancy within the assignment of data points to the workers and uses coding theoretic ideas so that the PS can recover $\nabla L$ exactly or approximately, even in the presence of stragglers. Communication-efficient gradient coding allows the workers to communicate vectors of length smaller than $d$ to the PS, thus reducing the communication time. While there have been schemes that address the exact recovery of $\nabla L$ within communication-efficient gradient coding, to the best of our knowledge the approximate variant has not been considered in a systematic manner. In this work we present constructions of communication-efficient approximate gradient coding schemes. Our schemes use structured matrices that arise from bipartite graphs, combinatorial designs and strongly regular graphs, along with randomization and algebraic constraints. We derive analytical upper bounds on the approximation error of our schemes that are tight in certain cases. Moreover, we derive a corresponding worst-case lower bound on the approximation error of any scheme. For a large class of our methods, under reasonable probabilistic worker failure models, we show that the expected value of the computed gradient equals the true gradient. This in turn allows us to prove that the learning algorithm converges to a stationary point over the iterations. Numerical experiments corroborate our theoretical findings.

</details>


### [188] [Energy Detection for Cognitive Radio with Distributional Uncertainty and Signal Variety under Nonlinear Expectation Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22659)
*Jialiang Fu,Wen-Xuan Lang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出基于非线性期望理论的广义能量检测模型，处理信号和噪声分布不确定性，使用G-正态分布描述噪声，信号幅值假设在有界范围内，推导最坏情况检测性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统能量检测方法将噪声不确定性视为噪声功率偏差，信号不确定性视为信号特性变化，使用概率方法并假设固定概率分布。实际场景中，由于概率模型不确定性和不同无线电技术接收到的信号显著变化，无线环境不仅存在分布不确定性，还有显著的信号多样性。需要更通用的理论框架处理这些不确定性。

Method: 基于非线性期望理论开发广义能量检测公式，使用G-正态分布描述信道噪声，假设传输信号随机变量的绝对值位于有界范围[σ_X, σ̅_X]内。最坏情况检测性能通过双重上确界（对所有可接受分布和所有可能信号实现）来表征，推导最小和最大检测错误概率的估计。

Result: 通过数值模拟验证了结果的有效性，提出的模型推广了经典能量检测理论分析，为分布不确定性下的鲁棒检测和信息论分析提供了潜在理论基础。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种处理信号和噪声分布不确定性的广义能量检测框架，基于非线性期望理论，使用G-正态分布和有界信号假设，推导了最坏情况检测性能界限，为认知无线电中的鲁棒检测提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Classical energy detection (ED) methods for cognitive radio (CR) have addressed noise uncertainty as deviations in noise power and signal uncertainty as variability in signal characteristics, which use probabilistic methods and assume fixed probability distributions for both. In practical scenarios, due to the uncertainty in probability models and the significant variation of primary signals encountered by receivers across different radio technologies, wireless environments exhibit not only distributional uncertainty but also substantial signal variety. In this paper, we develop a generalized formulation of energy detection based on nonlinear expectation theory, where both the signal and noise distributions are uncertain. We utilize the $G$-normal distribution to characterize channel noise. Moreover, to capture practical signal variety, the absolute values of transmitted signal random variables are assumed to lie within a bounded range $[\underlineσ_X,\overlineσ_X]$. The worst-case detection performance is then characterized by a double supremum, meaning over all admissible distributions and all possible signal realizations. We derive estimations for the minimum and the maximum detection error probabilities, and demonstrate the validity of the results through numerical simulations. The proposed model generalizes the classical theoretical analysis of energy detection and offers a potential theoretical foundation for robust detection and information-theoretic analysis under distributional uncertainty.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作为白皮书，本文采用愿景描述和分析方法：1) 概述统一编码方案的愿景；2) 探索6G通信场景带来的新编码挑战；3) 对潜在解决方案进行初步分析。

Result: 提出了为6G开发统一编码方案的具体愿景框架，识别了6G通信场景中信道编码面临的新挑战，并提供了初步的解决方案分析，为未来研究指明了方向。

Conclusion: 为满足6G系统的严格要求，需要开发一种多功能、统一的编码方案，该方案应具备竞争性纠错性能、低复杂度编解码能力，并能实现能效硬件实现。本白皮书为此愿景奠定了基础。

Abstract: The growing demand for higher data rates necessitates continuous innovations in wireless communication systems, particularly with the emergence of 6G. Channel coding plays a crucial role in this evolution. In 5G systems, rate-adaptive raptor-like quasi-cyclic irregular low-density parity-check codes are used for the data link, while polar codes with successive cancellation list decoding handle short messages on the synchronization channel. However, to meet the stringent requirements of future 6G systems, a versatile and unified coding scheme should be developed - one that offers competitive error-correcting performance alongside low complexity encoding and decoding schemes that enable energy-efficient hardware implementations. This white paper outlines the vision for such a unified coding scheme. We explore various 6G communication scenarios that pose new challenges to channel coding and provide a first analysis of potential solutions.

Abstract: In this paper, we establish a new law of large numbers with the rate of convergence for special partial sums in a probability space. The proof relies on nonlinear expectation theory, as the uncertainty of random variables in the special partial sums induces the sublinearity of the expectation. As an application, we apply the new theorem to analyze the feedback channel-based detection problem of non-i.i.d. input signals in communication systems. Specifically, we investigate the convergence rates of the upper probabilities of the detection errors within the sublinear expectation space.

### [191] [Ellipsoidal Manifold Optimization for Distributed Antenna Beamforming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23260)
*Minhao Zhu,Kaiming Shen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于黎曼流形优化的高效算法，用于解决具有每簇功率约束的下行分布式天线系统中的加权和速率最大化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式天线系统中，密集天线部署导致波束成形变量维度极高，同时多个独立的每簇功率约束增加了结构复杂性，使得传统的优化方法计算效率低下且难以扩展。

Method: 首先将低维子空间性质从总功率约束推广到每簇功率约束情况，证明所有驻点波束成形器都位于相应天线簇信道向量张成的子空间中。基于此将原高维约束问题转化为无约束的椭球流形乘积优化问题，系统推导了该流形的黎曼几何结构，并设计了专门的黎曼共轭梯度算法。

Result: 数值仿真表明，所提算法能达到与WMMSE方法和传统流形优化相同的局部最优解，但在计算效率和可扩展性方面显著优于基准方法，特别是在天线簇数量增加时优势更加明显。

Conclusion: 通过利用每簇功率约束下的低维子空间性质，将高维约束优化问题转化为黎曼流形上的无约束问题，所提出的黎曼共轭梯度算法在保持解质量的同时，大幅提升了计算效率和系统可扩展性。

Abstract: This paper addresses the weighted sum-rate (WSR) maximization problem in a downlink distributed antenna system subject to per-cluster power constraints. This optimization scenario presents significant challenges due to the high dimensionality of beamforming variables in dense antenna deployments and the structural complexity of multiple independent power constraints. To overcome these difficulties, we generalize the low-dimensional subspace property--previously established for sum-power constraints--to the per-cluster power constraint case. We prove that all stationary-point beamformers reside in a reduced subspace spanned by the channel vectors of the corresponding antenna cluster. Leveraging this property, we reformulate the original high-dimensional constrained problem into an unconstrained optimization task over a product of ellipsoidal manifolds, thereby achieving significant dimensionality reduction. We systematically derive the necessary Riemannian geometric structures for this specific manifold, including the tangent space, Riemannian metric, orthogonal projection, retraction, and vector transport. Subsequently, we develop a tailored Riemannian conjugate gradient algorithm to solve the reformulated problem. Numerical simulations demonstrate that the proposed algorithm achieves the same local optima as standard benchmarks, such as the weighted minimum mean square error (WMMSE) method and conventional manifold optimization, but with substantially higher computational efficiency and scalability, particularly as the number of antenna clusters increases.

</details>


### [192] [Index-Based Scheduling for a Resource-Constrained Quantum Switch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23476)
*Subhankar Banerjee,Stavros Mitrolaris,Sennur Ulukus*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出基于Whittle索引的量子交换机调度策略，优化有限量子内存下的多用户纠缠请求服务效率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子交换机需要利用有限的量子内存寄存器来服务多用户之间的纠缠请求，需要设计高效的调度策略来最大化服务效率

Method: 将调度问题建模为不安定多臂老虎机（RMAB）框架，证明可索引性，推导Whittle索引闭式解，将内存约束调度转化为0-1背包问题并用动态规划求解，提出两种低复杂度贪婪策略

Result: 证明了纠缠请求调度具有索引性，获得了所有请求-年龄对的Whittle索引闭式表达式，通过动态规划解决了内存约束调度问题

Conclusion: 提出的基于Whittle索引的调度策略能够有效利用量子交换机的有限内存资源，优化纠缠请求的服务效率，同时提供了低复杂度的实用解决方案

Abstract: We consider a quantum switch with a finite number of quantum memory registers that aims to serve multipartite entanglement requests among $N$ users. We propose scheduling policies that aim to optimize the average number of requests served per unit time by efficiently utilizing the switch's available memory. To measure the performance of the scheduling policies, we employ the newly introduced metric of age of entanglement establishment (AoEE). We formulate the scheduling problem in a restless multi-armed bandit (RMAB) framework. We show that the scheduling of entanglement requests is indexable. Subsequently, we find a closed-form expression of the Whittle index for all possible request-age pairs. By modeling the Whittle index of each request as its reward and its cardinality as its cost, we formulate the memory-constrained scheduling problem as a $0$-$1$ knapsack problem and solve it via dynamic programming. Furthermore, we consider two low-complexity sequential greedy policies that leverage two different modified Whittle indices.

</details>
